rgya gar skad du/ sar+b+ba ta thA ga ta tat+t+wa saM gra ha nA ma ma hA yA na sU tra/ bod skad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid bsdus pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ bam po dang po/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad thugs rje chen po de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje'i byin gyis brlabs dang / dam tshig gi ye shes rnam pa sna tshogs kyi khyad par dang ldan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rin po che'i dbu rgyan gyis khams gsum gyi chos kyi rgyal po dbang bskur ba mnga' brnyes pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rnal 'byor chen po'i dbang phyug // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi phyag rgya thams cad mnyam pa nyid du thugs su chud cing // thams cad kyi dgos pa mdzad pa nyid kyis/ sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa thams cad kyi re ba yongs su skong ba'i 'phrin las mdzad pa/ thugs rje che ba rnam par snang mdzad dus gsum du rtag par bzhugs shing // sku dang / gsung dang / thugs thams cad rdo rje lta bur gyur pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bzhugs shing bsngags bstod pa/ nor bu dang rin po che chen pos spras pa/ kha dog sna tshogs shing dril bu btags pa/ dar dang / 'phan dang / me tog gi phreng ba dang / rnga ma dang / dra ba dang / dra ba phyed pa dang / zla ba rlung gis bskyod pa rnams kyis mdzes par byas pa'i 'og min gyi lha'i rgyal po'i gnas na bzhugs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgu la 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje dang / kun tu spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang po dang / nam mkha'i snying po dang / rdo rje khu tshur dang / 'jam dpal dang / sems bskyed ma thag tu chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / nam mkha'i mdzod dang / bdud kyi stobs thams cad rab tu 'joms pa la sogs pa byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa dgu dang / gang gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ de yang 'di ltar 'dzam bu'i gling na de bzhin gshegs pa tshad med grangs med pa de dag gi skus kyang til gyi gang bu bzhin du gang bar snang ngo // de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku re re las kyang sangs rgyas kyi zhing grangs med tshad med pa rnams snang ngo // sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na yang chos kyi tshul 'di dag 'chad do// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad chen po/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad bzhin du rtag par bzhugs shing // sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje lta bur gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid du 'jug pas/ rdo rje dbyings thams cad thugs su chud pa'i ye shes sems dpa' nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo rdo rje'i byin gyis brlabs las byung ba'i ye shes kyi snying po/ de bzhin gshegs pa mtha' yas pa nyid kyi rdo rje chen po'i ye shes rin po che'i dbang bskur ba'i rin po che chen po/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du spros pa'i de bzhin nyid kyi ye shes mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pas byang chub par gyur cing // de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid dag pa'i phyir chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin dag par thugs su chud pa/ nam mkha'i khams thams cad du khyab pa'i gzugs thams cad du yang dag par ston pa/ mkhyen pas sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa'i khams rnams gdul bar spyod pa'i mchog tu gyur pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bka' nod cing don yod par mdzad pa nyid kyis thams cad dang mnyam pa med cing bla na med pa'i 'phrin las thams cad mdzad pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byang chub chen por sems brtan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad cad kyi rin po che'i dbang chen po bskur ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nyi ma'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bsam pa'i rgyal po yid bzhin gyi nor bu'i rgyal po'i rin po che'i dpal dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bzhad pa chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dag pa'i chos chen po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi shes rab chen po'i ye shes dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor lo dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dgongs pa 'chad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gdon mi za bar thams cad kyi dgongs pa mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi brtson 'grus chen po'i go cha shin tu brtan po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis srung zhing skyob pa'i gnod sbyin dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i phyag rgya bcings pa'i ye shes rnams so// kun bzang rab tu gdon mi za// bdud dang rab dgyes gtso bo dang // mkha' skyes shin tu gzi chen dang // rin chen dpal dang 'dzum pa che// kun tu gzigs pa'i dbang chen dang // 'jam dpal dkyil 'khor thams cad dang // mi gsung ba dang thams cad las// brtson 'grus ma rungs dam du gzung // rdo rje lcags kyu mda' gzhu dang // rin chen nyi ma rgyal mtshan 'dzum// pad+ma ral gri 'khor lo gsung // las dang go cha 'jigs byed bcings// thog ma tha ma med cing zhi// ma rungs khro bo bzod pa che// gnod sbyin srin po dam pa brtan// gzi chen dpa' bo dbang po che// u ma'i bdag po skye dgu'i mgon// gtogs 'dod rgyal 'dod thub pa che// 'jig rten skyong dang mkha' dang sa// 'jig rten gsum dang khams gsum pa// 'byung chen sems 'jig rten gsum rgyal bde spyod dang // bde spyod gtso bo rab 'dul mdzad// rdo rje gtso dang sa rab mchog // ye shes pha rol phyin pa'i tshul// byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par thar// de bzhin gshegs pa kha nang na bstan pa dang / phyir bstan pa bcings la rdo rje slob ma'i spyi bor bzhag ste 'di skad du brjod par bya'o// 'di ni khyod kyi rdo rje'i dam tshig yin gyis gal te 'ga' zhig la smras na/ klad pa 'gas par 'gyur ro// de nas dam tshig gi phyag rgya de nyid dang mna'i chu'i snying pos bsngags la slob ma de 'thung du gzhug go// de la mna'i snying po 'di yin te/ rdo rje sems dpa' deng khyod kyi// snying la yang dag gzhug par mdzad// gal te tshul 'di smras na ni// de ma thag tu dral te gshegs// oM badzrod ka tha/ de nas slob ma la 'di skad bsgos shig // deng phyin chad khyod kyi phyag na rdo rje nga yin gyis/ ngas 'di byos shig ces bsgo ba gang yin pa de bya dgos so// khyod kyis nga la brnyas par ma byed cig // mi bde ba ma spangs pas khyod dus byas nas dmyal bar ltung bar gyur ta re be sha aH/ de nas khro bos phyag rgya bcings la/ sems dpa'i rdo rje'i phyag rgya la mdud cing drangs la theg pa chen po mngon par rtogs pa'i tshig ci nus par smrar gzhug go// de nas phab ste babs ma 'dod na tshe 'di la// zhi ba dam pa mchog gyur pa// sangs rgyas nyid 'thob nges 'di bsgrub// ci ste mi 'dod dngos grub bzhin// phyag rgya chen po bcings nas kyang // de nyid chen po tshig re rer// brjod nas kun dang ldan par yang // thams cad bdag ni yin bsgoms na// ci ste 'dod na bdag nyid des// de bya gzi can dge ba yi// go 'phang tshe 'di nyid la 'thob// mi 'dod dngos grub gong ma bzhin// de nas dam tshig phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ ji ltar rdo rje 'dzin 'grub pa// de ltar bdag ces bsgoms na ni// sangs rgyas dang ni gzi chen 'thob// mi 'dod dngos grub gong ma bzhin// de nas chos kyi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ chos rnams thams cad rang bzhin gyis// dag ces brjod na nges par yang // sangs rgyas dang ni gzi can 'gyur// mi 'dod dngos grub gong ma bzhin// de nas las kyi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ thams cad kyi ni kun dag par// las rnams thams cad sbyangs na ni// sangs rgyas gzi can thob ci ste// mi 'dod dngos grub gong ma bzhin// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs dam pa'i dngos grub rnams so// de nas phyag na rdo rjes rang gi rig pa dam pa'i dngos grub kun gyi rgyud 'di gsungs so// dngos grub kun sbyor sangs rgyas kyi// bkas ni sems can kun don du// phyag rgya chen por bsgrub na ni// tshe 'di nyid la sangs rgyas 'grub// de nas dam tshig gi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad do// phyag rgya chen po'i tshul du ni// ji ltar rdo rje 'dzin grub pa// de bzhin bdag ces bsgoms na ni// skad cig gis ni gzi chen 'thob// de nas chos kyi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ yi ge med pa'i chos rnams la// rab tu spros pa yod min te// chos mchog 'di ni rjod byed cing // bsgoms na gzi can nyid du 'gyur// de nas las kyi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ dge ba'am yang na mi dge ba'i// gang gi las rnams byas pa ni// rgyal ba rnams la phul byas na// skad cig gis ni gzi can 'gyur// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes pad+ma'i rigs dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud 'di gsungs so// de la dang por ni phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ 'dod chags ngo bo nyid kyis dag // mu stegs can gyis mi gyur la// de la chags pa'i chos 'di ni// theg pa che la 'grub par 'gyur// de nas dam tshig gi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub ni 'di yin te/ ting 'dzin brtan pa'i tshul gyis ni// byams pa chen po bsgoms nas kyang // cho ga bzhin ldan khyab byas na// skad cig gcig gis gzi can 'thob// de nas chos kyi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ 'dod chags ngo bo nyid dag ces// smra bar gyur ba'i tshul 'di ni// 'dod chags pha rol phyin rnyed de// skad cig gis ni gzi can 'thob// de nas las kyi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de/ bdag gi lta dang reg pa dang // mnyan pa dang ni dran pa'ang rung // sems can rnams ni thams cad kyi// sdug bsngal kun gyi mthar phyin 'gyur// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes nor bu'i rigs kyi dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud 'di gsungs so// de la phyag rgya chen po dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud 'di yin te/ rdo rje snying po ji bzhin du// sangs rgyas kun dbang bdag gyur ces// bsgom par bya ba rnams bsgoms nas// skad cig gis ni gzi can 'thob// 'thob// de nas chos kyi phyag rgya dam pa'i dngos grub kyi rgyud bshad de// bdag nyid kyang ni spangs nas su// nor byin rab tu dga' byed cing // chos byung phyag rgya smra na ni// gzi can tshe 'di yang // bsgrubs na myur du 'grub par 'gyur// de la 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi dngos grub kyi rgyud do// rdo rje sems dpa'i phyag rgya che// bcings nas de yi mdun du yang // rdo rje sems dpa' bsgoms na ni// shin tu myur bar dngos grub 'gyur// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i rigs kyi dngos grub kyi rgyud do// rdo rje sems dpa'i ting 'dzin gyis// dam tshig gi ni mchog bcings na// rdo rje sems dpa' bsgoms na ni// nyi rim du ni dngos grub 'gyur// de la 'di ni pad+ma'i rigs kyi dngos grub kyi rgyud do// 'jig rten dbang po'i ting 'dzin gyis// chos kyi phyag rgya bcings nas kyang // 'jig rten mgon po bsgoms na ni// nyi rim du ni dngos grub thob// de la 'di ni nor bu'i rigs kyi dngos grub kyi rgyud do// rdo rje snying po'i ting 'dzin gyis// las kyi phyag rgya bcings nas ni// rdo rje snying po bsgoms na ni// nyi rim du ni dngos grub thob// rigs thams cad kyi dngos grub kyi cho ga rgyas pa'i rgyud do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes de bzhin gshegs pa thams ni mdun du yang // sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa bsgom// de nas de ma thag tu 'grub// ces sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs so// de la 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs la sogs pa'i dngos grub thams cad sgrub pa'i rgyud do// rdo rje bzlas pa'i tshul gyis ni// 'dod pa bdag ces bsgoms nas kyang // phyag rgya thams cad bsgrubs na ni// grub pa'i mchog ni kun bsgrubs pa'o// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas gsungs so// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i rigs kyi dngos grub thams cad sgrub pa'i rgyud do// bdag nyid nyid kyis rdo rje dbyibs// rab mnyam bzhag pas sgom byed cing // phyag rgya thams cad bcings na ni// de ma thag tu 'grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rjes gsungs so// de la 'di ni pad+ma'i rigs thams cad kyi dngos grub kyi rgyud de/ ye shes kun 'byung dngos grub kyi// pad+ma chen po'i rigs la gnas// bdag nyid kyis ni bdag nyid nyid// pad+ma'i dbyibs su bsgom par bya// zhes bcom ldan 'das kun du spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang pos gsungs so// de la 'di ni nor bu'i rigs kyi dngos grub thams cad kyi sgrub pa'i rgyud do// nor bu rin chen 'od zer 'bar// bdag nyid nyid kyis bsgoms na ni// nor bu chen po'i rigs mchod na// kun las 'byung ba'i dngos grub 'thob// ces bcom ldan 'das nam mkha'i snying pos gsungs so// rigs thams cad kyi dngos grub dam pa'i cho ga rgyas pa'i rgyud do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes de dbang phyag rgya ni// rab mnyam bzhag pas bcings nas kyang // snying ga mdzod spu mgrin spyi bor// bzhag nas sangs rgyas byin rlob bo// zhes sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs so// de la 'di ni de gi mtshan zlos pa// bsrung ba 'di ni rmad du che// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje chos kyis gsungs so// de la 'di ni nor bu'i rigs kyi bsrung ba'i dngos grub kyi rgyud de/ sangs rgyas sems can gtong byed par// ci nus par ni sbyor byed cing // nyi ma stong par mi bya bar// bsrung ba 'di ni rmad kyi mchog // ces bcom ldan 'das rdo rje bsrung bas gsungs so// rigs thams cad kyi bsrung ba'i dngos grub kyi cho ga rgyas pa'i rgyud de/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs kyi rgyud 'di bzhes par gsol/ gang gis sems can thams cad brtag pa thams cad kyi dbang phyug tu gyur nas rtogs par bgyi ste/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i slad du'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje la legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ phyag na rdo rje la legs par bshad pas nged kyis blangs shing byin gyis brlabs kyis legs so legs so// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gcig tu 'dus nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje la legs so zhes bya ba byin te/ rdo rje theg pa bla na med// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang // theg pa chen po mngon 'dus pa'i// mdo sde 'di ni legs bshad pa// legs so rdo rje sems dpa' khyod// rdo rje rin chen khyod legs so// rdo rje chos ni khyod legs te// rdo rje las ni khyod legs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid bsdus pa las brtag pa thams cad kyi thabs kyi cho ga rgyas pa'i rgyud rdzogs // // de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes de par bya'o// de nas zla ba'i mthar ting nge 'dzin de nyid kyis mtshan gcig thog thag tu bzlas par bya'o// de nas nam langs pa dang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad byon nas/ ci dga' ba bzhin du dbang bskur bar 'gyur ro zhes bcom ldan 'das nam mkha'i snying pos gsungs so// de nas las bsgrub pa bshad de/ de bzhin du bzlas la zla ba'i mthar mtshan gcig thog thag bzlas par bya'o// de nas nam langs pa dang bcom ldan 'das nam mkha'i snying pos don thams cad 'grub par 'gyur ro// de nas las thams cad byed par 'gyur ro zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pas gsungs so// nor bu'i rigs kyi nye bar sbyong ba'i cho ga rgyas pa rdzogs // // de nas rigs thams cad kyi thun mong du bsgrub pa'i yo byad dang cho ga rgyas pa ni 'di yin te/ de la dang por snying po thams cad kyi yo byad dang cho ga rgyas par bshad do// snying po bsgrub par 'dod na de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi grub par gyur cig ces brjod la snying po ci dga' bar bzlas shing bsgrub pa'i cho ga bya'o// de la 'di ni phyag rgya'i yo byad dang sngags ci dga' bar bzlas pa byas te 'di ni dngos grub bo// de la 'di ni rig pa'i yo byad dang cho ga rgyas pa ste/ kye sems can 'di dag thams cad ni ma rig pas ldongs par 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa bzlas pa'i cho ga rgyas pa rdzogs // // de nas rigs thams cad kyi thun mong du bsgrub pa'i cho ga rgyas pa ni 'di lta ste/ de la dang po kho nar de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi rigs kyi dngos grub ni 'di pa der phyag rgya bcings la rang gi ting nge 'dzin gyis gter gyi gnas der/ rdo rje blta bas blta ba na/ ci ste rdo rje lta bu yar bar mthong na/ de na gter yod par shes par bya'o// de nas rdo rje lcags sgrog gi dam tshig gi phyag rgya bcings te sa brkos la ji ltar dga' ba bzhin du blangs na rtsod pa med par thob par 'gyur ro zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas gsungs so// de la 'di ni rdzu 'phrul gyi dngos grub 'grub pa yin te/ phyag rgya gang sgrub par byed na badzra sid+d+hi zhes brjod par bya'o// rdzu 'phrul gyi dngos grub ni rnam pa bzhi yod de/ de ni 'di ltar chu'i steng nas phar 'gro zhing 'dug pa la sogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa la sogs pa thams cad kyi gzugs ston pa dang / ji srid du dga' ba de srid du mi snang bar 'gyur ba dang / nam mkha' la 'gro ba dang / dpag tshad stong gi steng du lding ba dang / 'og tu 'gro zhing 'ong ba dang / phyogs thams cad du dpag tshad stong du ci dga' bar song la bskor te slar 'ong ba dang / dpag tshad stong khor khor yug gi sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa shes pa dang / dngos po thams cad mig gis mthong zhing rna bas thos pa dang / phyogs thams cad du dpag tshad stong khor yug na gnas pa'i bud med thams cad ci dga' bar 'phang du blangs te 'dug pa dang / gser dang / nor bu dang / mu tig la sogs pa'i dbyig thams cad dang / nor thams cad phrogs nas kyang sus kyang cung zad kyang brgal mi nus te/ bdag gi rdo rjes kyang mi thub par 'gyur na/ gzhan gyis lta smos kyang ci dgos/ skyes bu stong phrag bcu bsdams pa'i stobs dang ldan pa dang / rtag tu nad med pa dang ldan pa dang / rtag tu 'dod pa thams cad longs spyod pa dang 'dzin gyis gsungs so// de la 'di ni dngos grub chen po 'grub pa yin te/ bdag nyid phyag rgya'i snying po don du bdag nyid kyis phyag rgya bsgrubs na sems dpa'i gzugs su gyur nas skad cig gcig gis rgyas pa'i rgyud rdzogs // // de nas rigs thams cad kyi thun mong gi gsang ba'i sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud yin no// de la 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi sku'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa yin te/ ji ltar de ltar 'dug nas kyang // skyil mo krung bcas bsgrub bya ste// ji ltar ri mo'i tshul byas nas// sems dpa' chen po grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas gsungs so// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i sku'i phyag rgya sgrub pa yin te/ ji ltar ri mo'i tshul du ni// brgyad bsgrub tshul du rab tu gnas// shin tu khros nas bsgrub byas na// the tshom med par 'grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje hU~M zhes bya bas gsungs so// de la 'di ni pad+ma'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i sku'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud yin te/ rdo rje skyil mo krung bcas la// lag gnyis rdo rje bcings nas kyang // ting nge 'dzin gyi sku gyur la// pad+ma 'byung ba bsgrub par bya// zhes bcom ldan 'das pad+ma'i sems dpas gsungs so// de la 'di ni nor bu'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i sku'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa yin te/ ji ltar 'dug gam nyal ba'am// 'chag kyang rung ste de ltar ni// rdo rje rin chen dbang bskur na// the tshom med par 'grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje snying pos gsungs so// de la 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs kyi gsang ba'i gsung gi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ lce rtse shin tu mi bsgul zhing // so dang mchu gnyis sbyar nas ni// rtog pa thams cad bsgrub bya zhing // sgra bral rdo rje'i tshig yin no// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gsung gis gsungs so// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i gsung gi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de// hU~M zhes bya ba 'brug sgrar bsgrags// khro bo'i ngag ni zab cing bstan// rdo rje chen po khro bo'i gsal// rdo rje khro bo'i gsung 'grub bo// zhes bcom ldan 'das rdo rje hU~M zhes bya bas gsungs so// de la 'di ni pad+ma'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i gsung gi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ dbugs mi 'byin ltar dbugs 'byin cing // phra ba'i tshig ni shin tu gsal// ting 'dzin ye shes snying po yis// zlos pa po rnams grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ting nge 'dzin gyi ye shes kyi snying pos gsungs so// de la 'di ni nor bu'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i gsung gi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ shin tu yongs su gsal tshig gis// rtag tu 'dud la brtson byed cing // tshul 'di bzlas par gyur na ni// myur du thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rjes gsungs so// de la 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i sems kyi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ rtag tu 'dod pa bcom ldan 'das// sems can thams cad bde sbyin pas// rdo rje sems dpa' bdag nyid du// bsgoms na myur du 'grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das 'dod pas gsungs so// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i sems kyi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ sems can kun la phan pa dang // ma rungs pa rnams gdul ba dang // sangs rgyas bstan pa bsrung ba'i phyir// khro bo dngos grub 'thob par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje hU~M zhes bya bas gsungs so// de la 'di ni pad+ma'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i sems kyi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ ji ltar pad+ma rab chags la// bsgos pa'i skyon gyis mi gos pa// de ltar bdag gis chags skyon yang // srid na chags pa de 'grub 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das pad+ma bzhad pas gsungs so// de la 'di ni nor bu'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i sems kyi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ nam zhig sems can thams cad kyi// dgos pa'i don ni kun sgrub cing // rin chen char ni 'bebs 'gyur zhes// grub na myur bar de 'grub bo// zhes bcom ldan 'das nam mkha'i snying pos gsungs so// de la 'di ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i rdo rje'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ ji ltar langs sam 'dug pa'am// 'chag kyang rung ste de ltar ni// lag pa g.yon pas phyag rgya mchog // thams cad byed na 'grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba phyag rgya rdo rjes gsungs so// de la 'di ni rdo rje'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i rdo rje'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ de lta de ltar gnas nas kyang // ji lta ji ltar byed kyang rung // rdo rje khro bo mdzub mo bcings// gos kyis g.yogs na 'grub par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi khro bo'i rgyal pos gsungs so// de la 'di ni pad+ma'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i rdo rje'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ lag ni g.yon pas pad+ma yi// khu tshur bcings te sbas nas ni// ji dgar myur du pad+ma yi// dngos grub kyang ni thob par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das kun du spyan ras gzigs kyi dbang pos gsungs so// de la 'di ni nor bu'i rigs kyi gsang ba'i rdo rje'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ g.yon pa'i rin chen khu tshur ni// bcings te dam pa'i lag g.yogs la// ci dga' bar ni rim gror byed// rin chen dngos grub thob par 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das nam mkha'i snying pos gsungs so// de la 'di ni rigs thams cad kyi gsang ba'i thun mong gi phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud de/ rang gi sems dpa'i ting 'dzin gyis// phyag rgya chen po'i tshul du ni// rdo rje dag dang rdo rje'i lta// ring por mi thogs mchog 'grub bo// zhes bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdo rje sems dpas gsungs so// rigs thams cad kyi gsang ba'i sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i phyag rgya bsgrub pa'i rgyud rdzogs sto// // de nas bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rjes de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad bos nas 'di skad ces gsungs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rtog pa 'di ni byin gyis brlab par mkhyen par mdzad du gsol// de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gcig tu 'dus nas yang legs so zhes bya ba 'di byin no// rdo rje'i theg pa bla na med// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang // theg pa chen po mngon 'dus pa'i// mdo 'di legs par bshad pas na// legs so rdo rje sems dpa' khyod// rdo rje rin chen khyod legs so// rdo rje chos khyod legs pa ste// rdo rje las ni khyod legs so// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid bsdus pa las rgyud thams cad kyi phyi ma'i phyi ma'i rgyud rdzogs // // de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje stan las langs te/ bcom ldan 'das la mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa 'dis gsol ba btab bo// rdo rje dbyings kyi sems dpa' che// sems can don mchog bdag nyid can// shAkya'i rgyal po ye shes che// rdo rje bdag nyid khyod phyag 'tshal// sems dpa' 'byung ba de nyid don// sems can rgyu ste tshul chen po// sems can don chen dgos pa'i don// sems dpa' sems dpa' khyod phyag 'tshal// sangs rgyas chos ni chos chen po// chos kyi 'khor lo rab skor ba// smra ba chen po rab rig mchog // sems dpa' chen po khyod phyag 'tshal// las chen bsrung ba chen po ste// las rnams thams cad rab sgrub pa// bdag nyid chen po 'gro spyod mchog // sems dpa' rgyu khyod phyag 'tshal lo// pha rol phyin pa kun brnyes pa// kun mkhyen ye shes mkhyen pa po// sems dpa' kun te thabs chen po// shes rab chen po khyod phyag 'tshal// thugs rje chen po mchog gi mchog // thugs rje thugs rje'i bdag nyid can// thams cad gtong ba byams pa che// kun mdzad khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// shAkya seng ge shAkya che// shAkya shAkya thub pa che// 'dul ba chen po khyab pa po// 'gro don 'dul mchog khyod phyag 'tshal// chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam brnyes pa// chos dbyings de bzhin gshegs pa ste// rdo rje mgon po mgon chen po// sems can tshogs ni khyod phyag 'tshal// 'od chen snang ba chen po ste// brtson 'grus chen po stobs chen po// dpa' bo chen po rab dpa' mchog // bde spyod dpa' bo khyod phyag 'tshal// tshangs pa rang 'byung bcom ldan 'das// shAkya dpa' bo thub pa che// kun bdag thub pa dag pa yi// chos rgyal khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// nam mkha'i sku ste sku yi mchog // sku gsum sku min sgom pa po// kun gyi sku ste sku che ba// rdo rje'i sku khyod phyag 'tshal lo// gsung min gsung ste gsung gi mchog // gsung gsum gsung min ston pa pa po// gsung kun shin tu gsung che ba// rdo rje'i gsung khyod phyag 'tshal lo// sems min sems te sems kyi mchog // sems gsum sems min ston pa po// thams cad sems te sems che ba// rdo rje sems khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rdor min rdo rje rdo rje'i mchog // rdo rje gsum pa rdor min sbyong // rdo rje thams cad rdo rje che// rdo rje rdo rje khyod phyag 'tshal// kun khyab srid pa'i rtse mo mchog // bde gshegs bdag po rgyal ba ni// khams gsum pa yi rgyal po che// snang mdzad khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad 'di dag ni// gang gis skad cig nyan byed dam// klog gam yang na sgom pa'ang rung // kun gyis sangs rgyas nyid thob 'gyur// mgon po khyod la gsol ba ni// sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir// thugs rje chen po bskyed nas kyang // chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor// de nas bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag pos bka' stsal pa'i tshig gsan nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la bos nas 'di skad ces gsungs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rnams yang gcig tu 'du bar mdzad par gsol/ de nas yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gcig tu 'dus nas tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// rtag par 'jig rten thams cad du// sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir// ji ltar 'dul ba sna tshogs pa'i// chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor// de nas 'di gsungs ma thag tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi mdun du rdul phra mo thams cad ji snyed pa'i dkyil 'khor kun du khyab par byas nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor bar gyur to// de nas yang byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// rtag par 'jig rten thams cad du// sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir// ji ltar 'dul ba'i sna tshogs pa'i// rdo rje'i 'khor lo rab tu bskor// de nas 'di gsungs ma thag tu de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul phra mo thams cad ji snyed pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams su/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje dbyings kyis rdo rje dbyings la sogs pa'i rdo rje'i 'khor lo thams cad rab tu bskor bar gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal bas de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// rtag par 'jig rten thams cad du// sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir// ji ltar 'dul ba sna tshogs pa'i// khro bo'i 'khor lo rab tu bskor// de nas 'di gsungs ma thag tu de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul phra mo thams cad ji snyed pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams su/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// rtag par 'jig rten thams cad du// sems can kun la phan pa'i phyir// ji ltar 'dul bar sna tshogs pa'i// pad+ma'i 'khor lo rab tu bskor// de nas 'di gsungs ma thag tu de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo ji snyed pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams su/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi rgyal pos pad+ma'i 'khor lo rab tu bskor bar gyur tshogs pa'i// nor bu'i 'khor lo rab tu bskor// de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi khongs su gtogs pa'i sems can phra ba'am/ sbom pa yang rung // de dag thams cad kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ri rab ri'i rgyal po rtse mo rdo rje dang / nor bu dang / rin po che las byas pa'i khang bu brtsegs par de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gdan la bzhugs nas/ rdo rje dbyings la sogs pa'i 'khor lo thams cad rab tu bskor bar phyogs kun nas mthong ngo // de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// mi yi nang du babs nas kyang // dgos phyir sems can kun gyi don// rdo rje'i 'khor lo mchog bskor zhing // mgon po rab tu bsgrub par mdzod// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis de bzhin gshegs pa la bos nas 'di skad ces gsungs so// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad yang gcig tu 'du ba mdzad du gsol/ de nas yang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gcig tu 'dus nas/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rnam par snang mdzad kyis de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rjer bdag nyid du gyur par mkhyen nas phyag na rdo rje la 'di skad ces gsungs so// rigs kyi bu khyed kyang nga'i thugs dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / rigs thams cad dang / dkyil 'khor thams cad dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs su zhugs shig // de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rjes de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snang bas tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// mdor na sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje ni// zhugs nas sems can thams cad la// phan pa'i phyir ni bsgrub par bya// de nas 'di gsungs ma thag tu 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na/ de bzhin gshegs pa ji snyed bzhugs pa rnams las/ de bzhin gshegs pa re res kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra mo dang mnyam pa'i sku 'phro ba mdzad pa rnams kyang // bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi thugs su zhugs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang / bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad kyi sku thams cad dang / gsung thams cad 'jug pa'i gnas dang / sems kyi rgyud 'byung ba thams cad dang / rdo rje'i tshul thams cad dang / yan lag dang / nying lag thams cad dang / gnas thams cad dang / mtshan thams cad dang / dpe byad bzang po thams cad dang / ba spu'i khung bu thams cad dang / rdul shin tu phra mo snyed kyi dkyil 'khor thams cad dang / thugs rnams su zhugs nas bzhugs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das yang dag par rdzogs par sangs rgyas nas ring por ma lon pa zhig na/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang / gsung dang / thugs rdo rjer de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad du bdag nyid gyur par mkhyen nas/ ri rab ri'i rtse mo nas snying po byang chub pa gang na ba der gshegs nas ched du bcom ldan 'das kyi byang chub kyi shing drung du 'jig rten pa dang mthun par bya ba'i phyir rtswa blangs nas ched du brjod pa 'di ched du brjod do// e ma sems can brtan pa yi// sems can don ni bdag don mchog // gang phyir gdul dbang brtan pa rnams// mu stegs lta bas gnas bar mdzad// mdor na mi 'dul 'jig rten pa// lta ba ngan pas ldongs pa rnams// ye shes snang bas dag bya'i phyir// sangs rgyas byang chub thob par 'gyur// de nas 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la de kho na nyid mi shes pas 'di skad du kye dge sbyong ji byang chub kyi phyir/ 'di lta bu'i sdug bsngal drag cing mi bzad pa la bzod par mdzad dam zhes gsol to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis rtswa de bting ste steng du bzhugs nas lha rnams la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// grogs po rnams/ kho bos byang chub thob par sgrubs shig // de nas 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha'i bu rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa'i don ma rtogs nas/ lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin gang na ba der dong nas ched du lha rnams kyi dbang po brgya byin la de ltar gyur ba 'di brjod do// de nas lha'i dbang po brgya byin gyis 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha rnams kyi tshogs kyis bskor te/ gzugs na spyod pa'i lha rnams kyi bdag po tshangs pa chen po la de ltar gyur pa 'di dag brjod do// de nas tshangs pa chen po 'dod pa na spyod pa dang / gzugs na spyod pa'i lha thams cad dang / lhan cig tu 'jig rten gsum po thams cad kyi bdag po dbang phyug chen po la de ltar gyur pa rnams brjod do// de nas 'jig rten gsum po mtha' dag gi bdag po dbang phyug chen pos lha rnams kyi bdag po mthu bo che la sogs pa la 'di skad ces smras so// grogs po rnams de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'jig rten dang mthun par mdzad cing // yang bla na med par yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub ston gyis/ 'di ltar 'jig rten na de bzhin gshegs pa ma yin no snyam du shes par ma byed cig // lha nyid las de bzhin gshegs par 'gyur gyis/ lha de dag nyid du bsgrub par bya'i/ de bzhin gshegs pa nyid du ni ma yin no// de legs kyis der mchod du 'dong bar sgrub bo// de nas lha thams cad kyi bdag po dbang phyug chen po la sogs pa snying po byang chub gang na ba dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying por byang chub par bzhugs pa gang na ba der dong nas/ ched du bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la thugs brtse bar dgongs te/ ran gyi gdan 'di las bzhengs la/ lha rdzas kyi gdan la bzhugs te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar mdzad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ lha'i bdag po de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// grogs po rnams/ kho bo la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub sbyin par sgrubs shig // de nas de dag gis 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag gis bstsal bar mi nus so// ci ste bdag cag gis nus par gyur na/ bdag cag nyid yang dag par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par 'gyur ro// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis don de nyid gsal bar mdzad cing // yang tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// de ni gzugs min gzugs min min// bden min min gtsang ba yi// sangs rgyas byang chub ye shes 'di// rtogs na rgyal ba nyid du 'gyur// de nas lha'i dbang po de dag gis cung zad cig cang mi smra bar gnas par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das rtswa'i gdan las bzhengs te/ lha de rnams la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// grogs po rnams/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes 'di lta bu rtogs par bya ba sgrubs shig // de dag gis gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das/ bdag cag gis rngo mi thogs so// de nas yang bcom ldan 'das kyis gdan de nyid la bzhugs bzhin du tshigs su bcad pa 'di gsungs so// yid kyis rab tu rtogs pas na// byang chub sems ni brtan par byos// sems dpa' rdo rje brtan byas la// sangs rgyas su ni bdag sgoms shig // de nas de dag gis 'di skad du/ de lta bu legs so zhes bya ba thams cad kyis smras nas dong ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mtshan mo de'i tho rangs 'jig rten dang mthun par bya ba'i phyir/ bdud sde dang bcas pa pham par byas nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su mngon par sangs rgyas nas/ sems can gyi khams ma lus shing lus pa med pa thams cad la phan par mdzad pa/ 'phags pa phyag na rdo rje rang gi thugs la zhugs pa la mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa 'dis mngon par bstod do// rdo rje sems dpa' sems dpa' che// theg pa chen po bdag nyid che// snang ba che zhing dag pa che// mgon chen khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje rgyal po rdo rje che// rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa kun// sems dpa' chen po brtson 'grus che// thabs chen khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje 'dod pa dag pa che// kun gyi bde ba bde ba che// bde mchog thog ma tha ma med// bzhad chen khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje legs pa dgyes pa che// legs zhes bya ba rab mnyes pa// mnyes pa che zhing dgyes pa che// rab dgyes khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje rin chen rgyal po che// dbang bskur bzang po bdag po che// rin chen thams cad mdzes pa che// rnam rgyal khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje gzi brjid gzi brjid che// 'od chen lham pa chen po ste// rgyal ba'i 'od de 'bar ba che// sangs rgyas 'od khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje rgyal mtshan dbal che ba// rgyal mtshan che bas nor rab gtong // nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan yu ba che// gtong ba'i rgyal mtshan khyod phyag 'tshal// rdo rje bzhad pa bzhad pa che// dgyes pa che zhing rab dgyes pa// dgyes pa'i shugs kyis rol cing dgyes// chos dgyes khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje chos ni chos che ba// sems dpa'i chos ni rab sbyong ba// sangs rgyas chos te chos rab mchog // 'dod chos khyod la phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje rnon po ral gri che// shes rab ye shes blo gros che// sdig gcod ral gri chen po ste// sangs rgyas mtshon khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje rgyu ste 'khor lo che// sangs rgyas 'khor lo gter chen po// dkyil 'khor kun te chos kyi mchog // chos kyi dkyil 'khor khyod phyag 'tshal// rdo rje gsung ba gsung ba che// spros med yi ge chen po ste// yi ge med pa bzlas pa che// sangs rgyas gsung khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje las te las rab mchog // las chen las rab byed pa ste// gsang ba'i mchod pa mchod pa che// sangs rgyas mchod khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje bsrung ba go cha che// go cha'i mchog ste brtan pa che// bsrung ba che zhing snying po che// sangs rgyas brtson 'grus phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje gnod sbyin khro bo che// ma rungs thams cad skrag byed pa// sangs rgyas kun gyi thabs chen te// bsrung ba mchog khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje bsdams pa phyag rgya che// dam tshig chen po bcing ba che// khu tshur chen po phyag rgya che// rdo rje khu tshur khyod phyag 'tshal// de bzhin gshegs pa phyag bya zhing // brjod de mchod de bsti stang bya// gang phyir thog ma tha ma med// byang chub sems ni khyod yin te// khyod la brten nas rgyal ba dang // dpa' bo byang chub sems dpa' kun// byung zhing yang dag 'byung 'gyur bas// sangs rgyas byang chub mchog gi rgyu// rdo rje sems dpa' khyod phyag 'tshal// rdo rje rin chen khyod phyag 'tshal// rdo rje chos khyod phyag 'tshal lo// rdo rje las ni khyod phyag 'tshal// yang dag par ni phyag 'tshal zhing // mtshan mchog gis ni khyod bstod pa'i// bsod nams gang yin de kun kyang // sangs rgyas byang chub thob par shog // mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad dam pa ni// rab dad pas ni lan cig tsam// gang gis legs par brjod pa ni// kun kyang sangs rgyas nyid du 'gyur// zhes sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs so// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje la de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad gcig tu 'dus te/ gsung gcig tu legs so zhes bya ba 'di byin no// rdo rje theg pa bla na med// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gsang // theg pa chen po mngon 'dus pa'i// mdo 'di legs par bshad pas na// rdo rje sems dpa' khyod legs so// rdo rje rin chen khyod legs so// rdo rje chos khyod legs pa ste// rdo rje las ni khyod legs so// bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dang 'phags pa byang chub sems dpar bcas pa rang gi thugs la zhugs pa thams cad dgyes shing mnyes nas bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpas gsungs pa la mngon par dgyes par gyur to// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid bsdus pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo rgyud nye bar bsdus pa dang bcas pa rdzogs // // rgyud 'di la 'gyur byang mi snang na'ang // paN+Di ta shrad+d+hA ka ra war+m+ma dang / bod kyi lo ts+tsha ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur bar grags//
